< date>
1385241886343< /date>
< Rating>
5</Rating>
< text>
I have a passion for watches,  as well as vintage pieces, rare artwork and antiques. I am a collector
of what I find interesting. In the past twenty-five years I must have visited over 150 Jewelry, Loan and Pawn shops in various states around the US and vintage boutiques in Europe.
From my first experience with the owner Yev Goldman and his entire staff, I have never been treated with a level of service which one would expect buying a 18k Gold Minute Repeater at the Vacheron Constantin Boutique on Rodeo or a 18K White Gold Paul Newman Daytona.
To call Yev's Jewelry & Loan a pawn shop, would belittle the boutique and the dedicated hard working staff. I have done both, purchased watches at a very fair price and loaned watches or other pieces in order to have immediate access to cash, if  exceptionally good deal on a watch or  collectors item was needed within hours. They have given me the opportunity to expand my collection at the best interest rates I have ever experienced. Most important is their integrity, they have educated me on pieces I overpaid and gave me advice not to purchase pieces that wouldn't hold value. I have never had a Jewelry or Watch store tell me that if I am buying a certain piece to re-sell at later time for a profit, not to do so, unless I truly liked the piece for myself and would keep it in my collection. Some of the Fancy Jewelry Stores in Beverly Hills that sell pre-owned refurbished watches or even new ones, should spend a day at Yev's to learn hospitality, service and most of all integrity.   Roman Okin</text>

< review>
The George, just might make me move from Chicago. I loved every aspect of this place. Came here for the weekend and my friends who live on the first floor housed me. I fell in love with the layout of the condo. Great space for them. 1 bed 1 bath + patio at a reasonable price. With everything being so new I loved the feel and the atmosphere. It is a great place to live, network, play and enjoy life. What creates such a great vibe is the rooftop. The pool is about the right size for a rooftop pool. The large hot tub is amazing, along side there is a small wadding pool/kids pool. There are chairs and beach beds for many people. The center of the pool area is the extremely large tv in the center. There is a party room that holds a pool table, ping pong table, foosball table, a very large dinner table, kitchen with a stove and fridge, large couches to hold at least 12 people. There is also an outdoor patio where there is a pour your own beer area. It has a great high end feel while it keeps things simple but elegant. The George is a lifestyle. One you will be very happy to live. I highly recommend this to be your place of living. Reach out to Laura for more information!< /review>

<Review>Rarely I leave a review after one visit, however this place is exceptional. The service is warm and the dining area is comfortable and calm. The food is meticulously prepared and so delicious it will be quite memorable. I had the Vietnamese rolls to start. They are served in a nice display and the taste is  top notch! I love Vietnamese food and found this to be one of the best rolls I've ever had. I would eat the peanut sauce on everything everyday if it were so possible! My entree is grilled pork with stir fried spinach, onion , cherry tomato side. You can taste the grill in the pork and the onions in a very good way. The spice level is perfect...enough to where you know it's there but not so much that it burns. It was such a perfect blend of flavor. If I lived nearby I'd eat here minimum weekly!
